# Azure Understanding The Big Picture

> This Azure fundamentals course is designed to give you a strong foundation in cloud computing, focusing specifically on Microsoft Azure services. Join instructor Walt Ritscher as he explores the big picture of cloud computing, including the benefits and different models like IaaS, PaaS, SaaS, and more. Learn how to navigate Azure, manage costs, and use the broad range of services available in Azur

> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017) | Beginner | 16K learners
> [Jump to Path Context ↓](#path-context)

## Instructor

- [[Learn-it Labs]]
- [[Walt Ritscher]]

## Skills Covered

- Microsoft Azure

## Table of Contents

>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/azure-from-a-10-000-foot-view?u=76281980&t=4)** If you are considering moving to Azure, you may feel overwhelmed since there is so much to explore, you've come to the right place as this course zooms out and looks at the big picture of Azure.

#### The fluctuating nature of the Azure portal
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Presenter] Before we go any further in the course, let's take a moment to appreciate the speed at which Azure Cloud tools improve every month.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=7)** The updates happen frequently.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=8)** New features appear when they're stable and ready to deploy.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=12)** Microsoft rolls out improvements in a continual stream.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=15)** Most of the time, this is a benefit to us.
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=17)** We get bug fixes and security updates in a timely manner.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=20)** We get to experiment with new tools as they are developed.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=24)** Of course, this means that the tools we use to interact with Azure must be updated to match the new features.
>
> **[0:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=29)** There will be new commands for the PowerShell API and the Azure web portal, UI gets updated every few months too.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=36)** That means that some of the examples in this course won't match the current Azure portal.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=41)** That's okay. Breathe deep.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=43)** Relax.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=44)** This is a big picture course.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=46)** We're here to look at the broad concepts of Azure and to explore the breadth of tools available in the Azure ecosystem.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=52)** While the portal UI might change, the concepts explained in this course will still be true.
>
> **[0:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=57)** So if you find yourself wondering why a menu is different, or a page seems to be misplaced, don't fret.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-fluctuating-nature-of-the-azure-portal?u=76281980&t=63)** Explore around.

### 1. The Big Picture

#### What is the cloud?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] I'll wager you're considering moving part of your assets to the cloud.
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=3)** You're not alone.
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=5)** The call of the cloud is loud and strong.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=7)** To start, it's a good idea to define some terms.
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=9)** What do people mean when they say the cloud?
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=12)** Perhaps you've heard the cynical answer, "It's just someone else's computer."
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=17)** That's a funny answer and there is a kernel of truth there, but nowadays, it's more complex than that.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=22)** Let's go back in time a few decades and look at a classic network diagram.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=27)** Despite the outdated appearance, these diagrams were useful for picturing how the network system was configured.
>
> **[0:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=33)** Typically, anything outside the company network, like the internet, was represented with the cloud icon.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=39)** You can see it in the lower right.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=41)** That tiny cloud in the network diagram, which once represented the services outside the company firewall, is now a multi-billion dollar industry.
>
> **[0:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=50)** Cloud vendors build every kind of service and offer it to us as cloud services.
>
> **[0:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=54)** To revisit the definition as defined by Microsoft, "Cloud computing is the delivery "of on-demand computing services over the internet," or the cloud.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=63)** The services offered by cloud vendors are extensive and varied.
>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=67)** How we think about the cloud is often tied to our jobs and needs.
>
> **[1:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=71)** Database admins think about renting database servers in the cloud.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=74)** Programmers think about setting up their build pipelines and source repositories in the cloud.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=79)** Data analysts want to leverage machine learning tools in the cloud.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=82)** Think about all the online services you use, Office 365, Google Sheets, OneDrive, Slack, Microsoft Teams.
>
> **[1:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=89)** Corporate purchasing departments think about buying these software suites that run in the cloud.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=94)** In other words, the services you find interesting will depend on your needs.
>
> **[1:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=98)** From our perspective, the cloud is a set of tools and services available from cloud providers like Amazon and Microsoft.
>
> **[1:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=105)** What about from their perspective?
>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=107)** They need to create services that customers want and keep them available at all times and ensure they are secure from threats.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=114)** For the vendors, cloud is a new way of thinking about system architecture, and the definition is refined every month.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=120)** There is plenty of thought given on cloud patterns, the best ways to build systems distributed across many data centers.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=126)** Cloud is a new way of thinking about massive scale of servers.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=129)** For the cloud providers, they need to figure out how to run systems with lots of servers.
>
> **[2:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=134)** It's not the same as having two server boxes in a closet.
>
> **[2:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=136)** For example, Azure has millions of servers deployed in data centers in every global region and available in 140 countries.
>
> **[2:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=144)** Consider how much work it is to provision and maintain this mountain of hardware.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=148)** The cloud is a new way of thinking about enormous network bandwidth.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=151)** For example, Azure has up to 1.6 million gigabits bandwidth per region.
>
> **[2:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=156)** Microsoft needs to figure out where to locate data centers for low latency and how to manage hardware for these massive workloads.
>
> **[2:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=163)** The cloud is a new way of thinking about virtualizing.
>
> **[2:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=166)** How do you virtualize network hardware in a way that makes sense for the cloud?
>
> **[2:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=170)** Or what about virtual machines?
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=172)** The cloud is a new way of thinking about selling hardware and software.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=175)** This is where it starts getting closer to us.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=177)** Should you buy 10 servers with Windows operating system and SQL Server licenses for each box, or should you lease cloud services to handle the hardware and licensing for you?
>
> **[3:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=186)** Now that we understand that the cloud is where we buy and use on-demand services, we should talk about the acronym aaS, which stands for as a Service.
>
> **[3:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=196)** There are three broad categories of cloud service.
>
> **[3:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=198)** Infrastructure as a Service, or IaaS, is an on-demand access to cloud-hosted physical and virtual servers, storage, and networking, the backend IT infrastructure for running applications and workloads in the cloud.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=213)** Software as a Service, or SaaS, is on-demand access to ready-to-use cloud-hosted application software.
>
> **[3:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=220)** Platform as a Service, or PaaS, is on-demand access to a complete ready-to-use cloud-hosted platform for developing, running, maintaining, and managing applications.
>
> **[3:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=232)** You'll find a discussion of these topics in the other videos in the course.
>
> **[3:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=236)** Let's continue our search for a useful cloud definition.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=238)** The US National Institute of Standards and Technology, or NIST, defines five essential characteristics of the cloud.
>
> **[4:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=246)** On-demand self-service is one.
>
> **[4:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=248)** This means the ability for an end user to sign up and receive services without the lengthy delays that have characterized traditional IT, and it also means that customers can change their levels of service through a dashboard without contacting the service provider.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=262)** Broad network access describes the ability to access the service via standard platforms, like desktop, laptop, and mobile.
>
> **[4:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=269)** These resources are also accessible from a wide range of locations, whether at work, or home, or on the road.
>
> **[4:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=275)** Resource pooling means that resources are pooled across multiple customers.
>
> **[4:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=280)** This reduces the cost for the cloud provider and the cloud customer.
>
> **[4:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=283)** I remember back in the early days of web hosting, you could lower the cost of web hosting by choosing a plan where your websites were hosted on the same server as other customers' websites.
>
> **[4:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=293)** This saved money for the customer, and the provider needed less hardware.
>
> **[4:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=297)** Rapid elasticity, this means the cloud features, or its capability can scale to cope with demand peaks.
>
> **[5:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=303)** In a sense, cloud computing resources appear to be infinite, or automatically available.
>
> **[5:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=308)** Finally, we have measured service.
>
> **[5:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=310)** Billing is metered and delivered as a utility service.
>
> **[5:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=313)** Features can be capped as needed for spending reasons, or capacity overloads.
>
> **[5:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=317)** For example, when a web API reaches 2 million calls, throttle the service to reduce costs.
>
> **[5:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=323)** NIST also defines the scope for cloud deployment, breaking the levels into private, public, and hybrid.
>
> **[5:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=328)** A discussion of what the various models mean will have to wait for another time.
>
> **[5:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=332)** For this course, I'm looking at the public cloud.
>
> **[5:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=334)** If you are interested in private, or hybrid, you'll be pleased to know that Azure can help you there too.
>
> **[5:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=339)** Most people can see the potential benefit of moving to the cloud.
>
> **[5:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=342)** I'll discuss some of those benefits elsewhere in this chapter.
>
> **[5:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=346)** To build a successful global cloud system that is robust, secure, and scalable is hard work.
>
> **[5:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=351)** Every cloud vendor has spent enormous amounts of time and money discovering the best ways to build modern systems.
>
> **[5:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=356)** That's a plus for us.
>
> **[5:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=358)** We can build on the shoulders of these giants.
>
> **[6:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=360)** Azure documentation is good with plenty of references material for the discussion of trade-offs and concerns of building a cloud system.
>
> **[6:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=368)** If you are a developer, I suggest you check out some of the architecture patterns that Microsoft uses in Azure.
>
> **[6:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=373)** You'll find more details at this URL.
>
> **[6:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=375)** So there you have a look at the ideals of cloud.
>
> **[6:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=378)** One final comment.
>
> **[6:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=379)** Moving to the cloud takes some effort and foresight.
>
> **[6:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=382)** You'll need to consider how the cloud affects your architecture.
>
> **[6:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=385)** Spend some time thinking about what parts of your system can stay on-premise, and what parts can be safely moved to Azure.

#### Benefits of using the cloud
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>

>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=7)** Cloud computing eliminates the capital expense of buying hardware and software.
>

>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=17)** Gone are the hours of managing racks of servers.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=20)** Plus, you stop managing the infrastructure.

>

>

>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=34)** You pay only for the compute power, storage, and other resources you use, with no long-term contracts or upfront commitments.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=40)** For example, I have a virtual machine that I use for teaching some of my courses.

>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=51)** The biggest cloud computing services run on a worldwide network of secure data centers, which are regularly upgraded to the latest generation of fast and efficient computing hardware.
>
> **[1:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=61)** This offers several benefits over a single corporate data center, including reduced network latency for applications and greater economies of scale.
>
> **[1:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=69)** The beauty of cloud computing is that the servers are off-premise, out of sight, and out of your control.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=74)** Suppliers take care of them for you and roll out regular software updates, including security updates, so you don't have to worry about wasting time managing the system yourself.
>
> **[1:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=83)** Most cloud vendors have service-level agreements, the contract that defines their offerings and limitations.
>
> **[1:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=88)** Part of the SLA is the availability level, their guaranteed service uptime, which typically is less than 1/10 of a percent.
>
> **[1:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=96)** You're paying for rock-solid uptime.
>
> **[1:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=98)** When there is an issue, say the cloud vendor backbone goes offline and affects service, you get automatic professional troubleshooting.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=106)** All the cloud vendors have contingency plans for failures, have redundant resources available to be activated in a crisis.
>
> **[1:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=112)** This is important for any organization, but especially for small businesses without the staff or deep IT knowledge to handle downtime.
>

>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=127)** All cloud providers offer a broad set of policies, technologies, and controls that strengthen your security posture.
>
> **[2:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=134)** Your data, apps, and infrastructure will be well-guarded from potential threats.
>
> **[2:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=139)** Their data center is going to have better access control than your suburban office space.
>
> **[2:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=144)** Plus, lost laptops are a billion-dollar business problem.
>
> **[2:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=147)** Losing the hardware is expensive.
>
> **[2:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=149)** Losing the sensitive data on the laptop drive is worse.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=152)** Because your data is stored in the cloud, you can access it no matter what happens to your machine.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=157)** Another benefit is scalability, which means that your resources can seamlessly increase or decrease in size or quantity.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=165)** For a startup, this could mean having one database server to start with and adding servers when business grows.
>
> **[2:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=171)** Elasticity is a similar benefit that is related to scalability.
>
> **[2:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=176)** It is the ability to grow or shrink infrastructure resources dynamically as needed, based on demand.
>
> **[3:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=183)** Scalability gives you the ability to increase or decrease your resources, and elasticity lets those operations happen automatically according to your configured rules.
>
> **[3:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/benefits-of-using-the-cloud?u=76281980&t=193)** In a sense, cloud computing resources appear to be infinite or automatically available.
>

>

#### What is infrastructure as a service (IaaS)?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] What comes to mind when you think of cloud?
>
> **[0:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=2)** For many people, especially in the IT world, infrastructure as a service is what they envision.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=7)** It's where Amazon made its cloud reputation with AWS and is a major part of how IT utilizes the cloud.
>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=14)** Infrastructure as service, or IaaS, is on-demand access to cloud-hosted physical and virtual servers, storage, and networking.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=22)** Think of it as the backend IT infrastructure for running applications and workloads in the cloud.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=27)** IaaS allows customers to instantly build out new hardware and other network devices.
>
> **[0:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=32)** Rather than doing it in-house, you have the IaaS provider provision the servers, virtual machines, hard drives, network switches, and firewalls.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=39)** IaaS is essentially outsourcing your computer infrastructure to the cloud.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=43)** With IaaS, you create your infrastructure out of rentable building blocks.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=47)** Each one is a separate service component that you can provision as needed and disable when you are finished.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=52)** Think about this.
>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=53)** When you buy an SSD drive for a server, you own that hardware even if it is only used for a few days.
>
> **[1:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=60)** With IaaS, you use the cloud disk, and when you're done, the cloud provider rents it to someone else.
>
> **[1:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=65)** With IaaS, you are out of the hardware business.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=68)** The cloud provider is responsible for the care and maintenance of all that equipment.
>
> **[1:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=73)** Traditionally, IaaS is about hardware, but as the cloud has grown, many providers offer other services that complement IaaS.
>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=79)** For example, customers often install databases or message queues on their servers, so it makes sense to make that easy to set up with your rented hardware.
>
> **[1:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=87)** This is not really IaaS, but the services are still useful.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=90)** Online dashboards are a big part of cloud services, and it's no different with IaaS.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=95)** Provision and manage your new infrastructure through the dashboard or via web-connected management tools on your local admin computer.
>
> **[1:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=103)** You still have responsibilities.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=104)** It's up to you and your organization to determine the system architecture.
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=108)** You have to configure the devices, buy software licenses, and install the software.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=113)** Because IaaS is mostly cloning of on-premise systems, there is a term, lift and shift, that is used to describe a common cloud pattern.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=120)** The lift and shift approach is a common migration option in which the enterprise moves in-house apps to the cloud without redesign.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=127)** Your apps and systems stay the same.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=129)** You just rehost them in the cloud system.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=132)** This lift and shift approach is nice.
>
> **[2:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=133)** Since you're trading your in-house hardware for similar cloud devices, you should be able to transition your custom application to the new environment with minimal changes to the application code.
>
> **[2:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=143)** There are some additional benefits.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=145)** You get the economies of scale, easily add hardware as demand increases.
>
> **[2:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=149)** How good are your on-premise monitoring and analysis tools?
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=153)** It's a sad truth that many organizations are information-poor regarding what is happening in the data center.
>
> **[2:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=158)** This is especially true for small businesses.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=161)** But with the cloud, monitoring is baked into the system.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=165)** Guess what?
>
> **[2:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=166)** Hardware is a commodity, and that means that the same categories of hardware are available from any IaaS cloud provider.
>
> **[2:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=171)** Should it be necessary to change providers, it's easier to transition.
>
> **[2:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=176)** Cost savings are a big selling point for cloud services, and it's the same for IaaS.
>
> **[2:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=179)** Think how much money you can save on the cost of setting up a new data center.
>
> **[3:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=183)** You still have direct access to the servers.
>
> **[3:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=185)** You can remote desktop connect to the computers and manage it in familiar ways.
>
> **[3:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=189)** You maintain complete control over your data.
>
> **[3:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=191)** This could be very important for your quirky in-house point-of-sales app that needs special attention from your data people.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=197)** This bears repeating.
>
> **[3:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=199)** Deploying new infrastructure is fast.
>
> **[3:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=200)** You can add hardware much faster than doing so in your own data center, and that makes IaaS terrific for testing new ideas.
>
> **[3:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=207)** Say you have an idea for a new switching and firewall system.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=210)** Spin up some rented equipment, test your ideas, and dismantle the system when done.
>
> **[3:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=215)** There are plenty of IaaS providers available for your needs.
>
> **[3:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=218)** Here's a short list of well-known providers.
>
> **[3:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=221)** Some examples of what you can do in Azure, you can create Azure virtual machines with either Windows or Linux operating systems.
>
> **[3:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=227)** You can provision hard disks for the VMs and set up cloud file shares.
>
> **[3:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=231)** When it comes to networking, there are a bunch of choices, too, from virtual networks to DNS, from load balancers to content delivery networks.
>
> **[4:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=240)** Azure has a complete list of infrastructure waiting for you to deploy.
>
> **[4:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-infrastructure-as-a-service-iaas?u=76281980&t=244)** We'll explore more as we go through the course.

#### What is software as a service (SaaS)?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Software as a service, S-A-A-S, or SaaS, is a hugely successful part of cloud computing.
>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=6)** It is on demand access to ready-to-use, cloud-hosted application software.
>
> **[0:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=11)** Think of it as a subscription based model where the software is hosted in the cloud and accessed via the internet.
>
> **[0:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=17)** Keeping your family pictures in Google Photos is a smart use of a cloud service, so is saving your Garden Club files on Dropbox or OneDrive.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=24)** Your files are safely stored in another location accessible from many devices and locations.
>
> **[0:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=29)** They are easy to share with other people, and the cloud service manages backups and security.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=34)** Software as a service is a way of defining centrally hosted applications over the internet as a service.
>
> **[0:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=40)** SaaS applications are sometimes called on-demand software, web-based software, or hosted software.
>
> **[0:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=46)** For most SaaS applications, you simply access it via the internet, usually through a browser.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=51)** There is no need to download or install anything on the client computer.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=55)** While the browser is a popular way to access SaaS applications, they often have native clients too.
>
> **[1:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=60)** For example, Microsoft OneDrive has a website and a sync client.
>
> **[1:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=65)** The sync client ensures the files are available on your local computer or mobile device, but the key is that the file management is in the cloud.
>
> **[1:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=72)** With SaaS, the cloud provider creates the software application.
>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=75)** Often they add features that help customers collaborate.
>
> **[1:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=78)** You see this in how Google Sheets enables multiple people to simultaneously edit the sheet at the same time.
>
> **[1:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=84)** SaaS is a huge and growing market.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=86)** Office software is the best example of businesses utilizing SaaS.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=90)** There are packages for every type of office work, office productivity tools, accounting, invoicing, sales, and planning.
>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=97)** There are apps for communication with people and scheduling online meetings.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=101)** You'll find sales, tools, and apps that help you manage your financial information.
>
> **[1:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=105)** Plus, there are applications for using your calendar and files online.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=109)** Not only do cloud providers create the applications, they also manage all the technical details.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=113)** They manage the data.

> **[1:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=115)** They are responsible for the hardware too.
>

>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=123)** Let's compare the traditional approach to software against the SaaS approach.
>
> **[2:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=127)** on-premise software is typically purchased to a perpetual license, which means buyers own a license for the software.
>
> **[2:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=133)** They also pay 15 to 20% per year in maintenance and support fees.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=137)** SaaS, on the other hand, allows buyers to pay an annual or monthly subscription fee, which typically includes the software license, support, and most other fees.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=145)** A key benefit of SaaS is being able to spread out cost over time.
>
> **[2:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=149)** On-premise software is installed on the client computer.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=152)** This is often managed by IT policies where standard images of purchase software is pushed to the computers.
>
> **[2:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=158)** In SaaS, it's installed through the subscription tool or accessed online.
>
> **[2:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=162)** In on-premise, there must be a compliance check to verify that the organization is using licenses correctly.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=168)** When you have a 50 seat license, you can't have 75 employees using the software.
>
> **[2:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=173)** In SaaS, the compliance is much easier.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=175)** If an employee is subscribed, they have access.
>
> **[2:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=178)** It's to add or remove subscriptions through the online dashboard.
>
> **[3:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=182)** In the traditional approach, data and files are stored on the local user computer or on a shared drive.
>
> **[3:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=188)** SaaS applications are updated and used online with file saved in the cloud rather than on individual computers.
>
> **[3:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=194)** There are more benefits, no initial setup costs.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=197)** Applications are ready to use once the user subscribes, pay for only what you use.
>
> **[3:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=201)** This is beneficial when something is only required for a short period.

>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=210)** Applications can be accessed via any internet capable device, such as desktops, smartphones, and tablets.

>
> **[3:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=222)** This is good for remote workers and a prime reason that companies are able to hire and retain talent outside of the company offices.

> **[4:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=286)** LinkedIn Sales Navigator is an advanced sales tool that aids sales teams, organizations, and individuals to build and nurture customer relationships on the network.
>
> **[4:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=297)** LinkedIn recruiter is the platform for finding, connecting with and managing job candidates.
>
> **[5:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=302)** Finally, there is LinkedIn Learning.
>
> **[5:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=304)** This definitely fits the software as a service model.
>
> **[5:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=307)** The SaaS market continues to grow quickly because it solves a real need for many organizations.
>
> **[5:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-software-as-a-service-saas?u=76281980&t=312)** In many areas, it has become the preferred delivery model and is the largest segment of the cloud market.

#### What is platform as a service (PaaS)?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Platform as a Service, or PaaS, is a relatively new but rapidly growing segment in cloud computing.
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=7)** It provides an easy approach for accessing a development-rich environment for building applications.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=12)** It simplifies the development process by providing a complete, ready to use environment in the cloud.
>
> **[0:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=19)** This allows developers to focus on their work without managing the underlying infrastructure.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=24)** A development platform is a comprehensive set of tools, services, and infrastructure that provides developers with the necessary resources to build, test, deploy, and manage software applications efficiently.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=36)** A comprehensive platform includes many useful parts.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=39)** What's part of the platform varies depending on the programming language and the application type, but typically it includes the following components, hardware, operating systems, development tools, middleware, frameworks, and runtime environments.
>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=53)** Platform as a Service offers several advantages.
>
> **[0:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=56)** It has a simplified development, it provides all tools and services needed to build and deploy applications in one integrated platform, its cost efficiency reduces the need for extensive hardware and software setup and maintenance.
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=68)** focus on productivity.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=70)** Developers can concentrate on coding and innovation rather than infrastructure management.
>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=75)** Plus, it easily scales applications to meet the demand without worrying about underlying infrastructure.
>
> **[1:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=80)** Let's take a look at the target audience.
>
> **[1:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=81)** Platform as a Service is primarily designed for developers to build and deploy applications efficiently for operations professionals to manage and maintain applications without dealing with hardware.
>
> **[1:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=92)** As far as the end user is concerned, they interact with the applications built and deployed, but they do not engage with the platform directly.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=99)** Unlike traditional development methods that require extensive setup and maintenance of hardware and software, Platform as a Service provides everything needed to build and run applications in a single integrated platform.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=110)** Another way of saying this is Platform as a Service provides ready-made services for your application rather than making you assemble the right software environment, for example, creating a virtual machine image, choosing the right run times, configuring networks, installing the developer tools and frameworks.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=126)** The platform offers scale out services that are ready to use.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=129)** Like Infrastructure as a Service, Platform as a Service includes infrastructure.
>
> **[2:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=134)** The hardware is there.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=135)** In a sense, you are still renting the devices, but you don't manage them in the same way.
>
> **[2:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=140)** Instead, they are configured and managed by the platform provider.
>
> **[2:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=143)** Since it is targeted as simplifying application development, it's not surprising to find that it includes lots of services that complement development.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=151)** For example, you might get development tools and IDEs, business intelligence services and app analytics, and don't forget databases.
>
> **[2:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=159)** It often includes DevOps tools that support the entire application lifecycle from development to deployment, testing and maintenance, and working with source control.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=168)** This integration streamlines processes and enhances productivity.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=172)** Let's do a comparison between the traditional method and the more modern Platform as a Service.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=177)** Both these approaches have their advantages and challenges.
>
> **[3:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=181)** The traditional approach offers high-customization and control.
>
> **[3:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=184)** In the Platform as a Service, there's limited customization due to standardized environments.
>
> **[3:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=189)** In traditional, there can be significant upfront costs, also called CapEx, high initial investment in hardware and software, whereas Platform as a Service is more cost effective.
>
> **[3:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=200)** It's basically a subscription-based pricing with no large initial investment.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=205)** In traditional, you have ongoing maintenance, continuous need for updates, repairs, and security management.
>
> **[3:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=211)** Whereas Platform as a Service, the provider handles all the maintenance updates and security.
>
> **[3:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=216)** With traditional, you may have time-consuming setup.
>
> **[3:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=219)** You have to set up and configure environments that can delay project start times.
>
> **[3:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=223)** To be clear, this is becoming less of an issue due to the rise of customizable virtual machines and containers.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=229)** Whereas in Platform as a Service, we've got these ready to use environments that enable faster project starts.
>
> **[3:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=235)** There are plenty of providers available for your needs.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=238)** Here is a short list of well-known providers.
>
> **[4:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=241)** To sum up what we've seen, cloud platform services try to make it simpler to build and deploy applications.
>
> **[4:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-platform-as-a-service-paas?u=76281980&t=247)** They offer platforms upon which apps and services can be built.

#### What is services as a service (SEaaS)?
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Earlier in this course, we looked at SaaS, or software as a service.
>
> **[0:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=3)** Recently, there is another kind of service being offered that has the same acronym, it's services as a service.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=10)** That's confusing, don't you think?
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=12)** So let's invent a new acronym for this course to aid in the discussion.
>
> **[0:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=15)** we'll call it SEaaS, S-E-A-A-S.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=18)** These are typically web services that provide a specific and narrow set of behaviors and data.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=23)** They are not standalone.
>
> **[0:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=25)** They are meant to be part of a larger application.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=28)** For example, we might have address verification or phone validation or a tax rate calculator, or an SMS provider.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=35)** Many of the vendors that provide these web services are companies that also provide software as a service.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=41)** So these SaaS providers created an email validation for their application, then they sell the email validation service to other software companies.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=49)** That's the services as a service.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=52)** This is a growing segment of cloud.
>
> **[0:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/what-is-services-as-a-service-seaas?u=76281980&t=53)** Usually you'll see them listed as commercial web services you can use from your own application.

>

>

>
> **[1:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/subscription-choices-for-azure?u=76281980&t=97)** Microsoft Azure for government is certified to meet these requirements.
>
> **[1:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/subscription-choices-for-azure?u=76281980&t=101)** It does this through multiple avenues, including using a separate physical and network-isolated instance of Azure for each agency.
>

>

>

> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/subscription-choices-for-azure?u=76281980&t=148)** With the annual Azure grant, you get a generous amount of service free every year.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/subscription-choices-for-azure?u=76281980&t=152)** That means you won't owe any money to Microsoft unless you exceed the grant limit.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/subscription-choices-for-azure?u=76281980&t=157)** If you are a current full-time STEM student or faculty in an accredited, degree-granting four-year educational institution, you can get a free Azure subscription.

#### Understand Azure costs and fees

> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=172)** So you can see here we've got Azure database from MySQL, we have Azure SQL, we have Azure SQL Databases, and then we've got Microsoft's Azure Cosmos DB, which is their fast NoSQL database.
>
> **[3:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=185)** We've looked at developer tools.
>
> **[3:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=186)** Let's talk about DevOps.
>
> **[3:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=188)** DevOps are tools to help developers write, deploy, test, run, and maintain applications.
>
> **[3:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=192)** So here we've got Azure Boards for planning and tracking work, Azure Artifacts for hosting and creating and sharing packages with your team.
>
> **[3:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=201)** We've got Azure Pipelines for continuously building, testing, and deploying to any platform and cloud.
>
> **[3:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=207)** Got Azure Test Plans for testing and shipping with confidence, and Azure Repos, which is an alternative to GitHub Repos.
>
> **[3:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=214)** Internet of Things, or IoT, is a collection of services that connect and control IoT devices.
>
> **[3:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=220)** Azure IoT supports a large range of devices including industrial equipment, microcontrollers, and sensors.
>
> **[3:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=227)** Those IoT devices then communicate with the Cloud IoT and other services, which then process the device data to monitor and manage devices.
>
> **[3:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=235)** In media, we have tools for working with media, like we can encode the media using media services.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=242)** We can encode it and store it and stream either video or audio.
>
> **[4:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=245)** If you need a player to look at these media items, then you can use the Azure Media Player.
>
> **[4:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=251)** There's also the Content Delivery Network for making sure that your content has a reliable content delivery across the globe.
>
> **[4:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=258)** In migration, there are tools to migrate your existing systems to Azure.
>
> **[4:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=262)** You can find them here.
>
> **[4:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=264)** Let's look at mixed reality next.
>
> **[4:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=265)** These cloud services like Azure Remote Rendering and Azure Spatial Anchors help developers build immersive experiences on a variety of platforms.
>
> **[4:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=275)** These services allow you to integrate spatial awareness into your projects, like that's what you do here, multi-user, spatially aware, mixed reality experiences.
>
> **[4:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=282)** Here we've got Digital Twins, which is using IoT spatial intelligence.
>
> **[4:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=287)** And then for rendering, you can render high quality interactive 3D content and then stream it to your mixed reality devices.
>
> **[4:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=294)** In the mobile world, we have services that help you work in mobile applications.
>
> **[4:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=299)** Most of these are not for creating the mobile applications.
>
> **[5:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=302)** The only exception here is the Xamarin, but these are things like Azure Maps and App Service and API Management.
>
> **[5:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=308)** These are tools that you might call from your mobile application into the cloud service.
>
> **[5:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=312)** Azure provides a wide range of networking tools and capabilities.
>
> **[5:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=316)** So you've got Azure DNS, you've got Azure Firewall.
>
> **[5:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=319)** There are things like load balancers, traffic managers, virtual networks, VPN gateways, and many more.
>
> **[5:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=327)** Now in security, you can find all these services to help secure your cloud applications, including Azure Active Directory.
>
> **[5:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=335)** We see that here, and we also have things like Microsoft Sentinel and Microsoft Defender for IoT and Microsoft Defender for Cloud.
>
> **[5:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=343)** In the storage world, we have services to handle the modern data storage needs.
>
> **[5:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=348)** There are many different storage types.
>
> **[5:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=350)** For instance, there is something called blob storage.

>
> **[5:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=354)** We have regular storage, we have queue storage, we have disk storage, and there's also in here is the Data Lake storage, Azure Backup.
>
> **[6:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/azure-understanding-the-big-picture-24392017/the-broad-world-of-azure-services?u=76281980&t=365)** What about this virtual desktop infrastructure?
>
